     8→
     9→## Setup
    10→
    11→```bash
    12→npm install
    13→npx playwright install chromium
    14→```

    16→---
    17→
    18→## Running Tests
    19→
    20→### Full gate (smoke → regression → critical)
    21→
    22→```bash
    23→npx playwright test
    24→```
    25→
    26→### By tier
    27→
    28→```bash
    29→npm run test:smoke       # Fast smoke (8 tests, ~15s)
    30→npm run test:regression  # Full regression suite
    31→npm run test:critical    # Critical loop integrity
    32→```
    33→
    34→### Specific spec files
    35→
    36→```bash
    37→# M1 debug dashboard
    38→npx playwright test tests/regression/m1-debug-dashboard.spec.js
    39→
    40→# M1 activity duration + AI cycle
    41→npx playwright test tests/regression/m1-activity-duration.spec.js
    42→
    43→# Slot system / capacity
    44→npx playwright test tests/regression/slot-system.spec.js

    48→

    50→npx playwright test tests/regression/fallback-logic.spec.js

    64→|---------|---------|----------|
    65→| `BASE_URL` | `https://ai-aquarium-phaser.vercel.app` | `.env` file or env var |

    67→| Retries | 1 | `playwright.config.js` |

    77→## Test Structure
    78→
    79→```
    80→tests/
    81→├── helpers.js                          # Shared helpers (waitForEngine, pollEngineState, waitForDashboard)
    82→├── smoke/
    83→│   └── app-loads.spec.js               # Page loads, engine init, 3 characters, 10 objects
    84→├── regression/
    85→│   ├── ai-decisions.spec.js            # AI LLM requests, valid action types, 30s interval, dialogue fields
    86→│   ├── character-movement.spec.js      # A* pathfinding, tile movement, bounds check
    87→│   ├── character-facing.spec.js        # FRG-244: facing toward objects + characters during talk
    88→│   │                                   #   (runs against local dev server at localhost:5173)
    89→│   ├── walk-animation.spec.js          # FRG-204: walk animation stutter/freeze fix
    90→│   │                                   #   moveTo resets walk state, large-delta frame accumulation,
    91→│   │                                   #   full 4-frame cycle, walkTimer remainder invariant
    92→│   │                                   #   (runs against local dev server at localhost:5174)
    93→│   ├── contextual-interaction-animations.spec.js  # FRG-243: contextual anim per object type,
    94→│   │                                   #   spriteKey/interactAnim during+after interaction, live sim,
    95→│   │                                   #   all 9 interaction sprites (runs against localhost:3000)
    96→│   ├── object-interaction.spec.js      # Object state transitions, debug panel
    97→│   ├── speech-bubbles.spec.js          # Dialogue lines, pendingSpeech, speech timer
    98→│   ├── m1-debug-dashboard.spec.js      # Debug page layout, real-time updates, pause/resume,
    99→│   │                                   #   position/facing/target fields, reset behavior, speed controls
   100→│   ├── m1-activity-duration.spec.js    # Activity timers, 30s AI cycle, action types
   101→│   ├── slot-system.spec.js             # Slot/capacity display, pip indicators, reservations,
   102→│   │                                   #   multi-capacity simultaneous use (kotatsu/tv)
   103→│   ├── talk-handshaking.spec.js        # TALK/REJECT events, talking state, canTalk filter
   104→│   └── fallback-logic.spec.js          # FALLBACK events, plan changes, reservation release
   105→└── critical/
   106→    └── sim-loop-integrity.spec.js      # End-to-end: LLM → move → object change → no errors
   107→```

   136→---
   137→
   138→## CI (GitHub Actions)
   139→
   140→Tests run automatically on every push and pull request via `.github/workflows/playwright.yml`.
   141→
   142→Results are stored as artifacts (JSON report + test-results folder).
   143→
   144→To run CI locally with the same config:
   145→
   146→```bash
   147→npm ci
   148→npx playwright install --with-deps chromium
   149→npx playwright test
   150→```
   151→
   152→---
   153→
   154→## Known Issues
   155→
   156→| Issue | File | Notes |
   157→|-------|------|-------|
   158→| `talk` action rarely observed in short runs | `talk-handshaking.spec.js` | AI is non-deterministic; tests gracefully skip if not observed |
   159→| REJECT events are probabilistic | `talk-handshaking.spec.js` | Only fires when two characters attempt simultaneous talk |
   160→| FALLBACK events require 30s+ observation | `fallback-logic.spec.js` | Events appear after AI cycle + object contention |
   161→| Sim clock ratio ~36x in headless (vs 60x in browser) | `critical/sim-loop-integrity.spec.js` | RAF throttled in headless — documented, not a product bug |
   162→

     1→'use strict';
     2→/**
     3→ * Shared helpers for AI Aquarium QA tests.
     4→ * All tests run against the deployed BASE_URL via window._gameEngine.
     5→ */
     6→
     7→/**
     8→ * Wait for Phaser to finish booting and the SimulationEngine to be attached.
     9→ * @param {import('@playwright/test').Page} page
    10→ * @param {number} [timeout=20000]
    11→ */
    12→async function waitForEngine(page, timeout = 20_000) {
    13→  await page.waitForFunction(
    14→    () => window._gameEngine &&
    15→          window._gameEngine.characters &&
    16→          window._gameEngine.characters.length === 3,
    17→    { timeout }
    18→  );
    19→}
    20→
    21→/**
    22→ * Read the live engine state.
    23→ * @param {import('@playwright/test').Page} page
    24→ */
    25→async function getEngineState(page) {
    26→  return page.evaluate(() => {
    27→    const eng = window._gameEngine;
    28→    return {
    29→      simTime: eng.getSimTimeString(),
    30→      aiEnabled: eng.aiEngine?.enabled ?? false,
    31→      characters: eng.characters.map(c => ({
    32→        name: c.name,
    33→        label: c.label,
    34→        tx: c.tx,
    35→        ty: c.ty,
    36→        action: c.action,
    37→        mood: c.mood,
    38→        energy: c.energy,
    39→      })),
    40→      objectStates: eng.objectEngine.getAll().map(o => ({
    41→        id: o.id,
    42→        label: o.label,
    43→        state: o.state,
    44→      })),
    45→    };
    46→  });
    47→}
    48→
    49→/**
    50→ * Poll engine state until predicate returns truthy, or timeout.
    51→ * @param {import('@playwright/test').Page} page
    52→ * @param {(state: object) => boolean} predicate
    53→ * @param {number} [timeoutMs=30000]
    54→ * @param {number} [intervalMs=500]
    55→ */
    56→async function pollEngineState(page, predicate, timeoutMs = 30_000, intervalMs = 500) {
    57→  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs;
    58→  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
    59→    const state = await getEngineState(page);
    60→    if (predicate(state)) return state;
    61→    await page.waitForTimeout(intervalMs);
    62→  }
    63→  throw new Error(`pollEngineState timed out after ${timeoutMs}ms`);
    64→}
    65→
    66→/**
    67→ * Wait for /debug.html dashboard to finish loading.
    68→ * Shared by m1-debug-dashboard, slot-system, talk-handshaking, fallback-logic specs.
    69→ * @param {import('@playwright/test').Page} page
    70→ * @param {number} [timeout=20000]
    71→ */
    72→async function waitForDashboard(page, timeout = 20_000) {
    73→  await page.waitForSelector('#characters-grid', { timeout });
    74→  await page.waitForSelector('#event-log', { timeout });
    75→  await page.waitForFunction(
    76→    () => {
    77→      const cards = document.querySelectorAll('[id^="char-"]');
    78→      if (cards.length < 3) return false;
    79→      return cards[0].textContent.includes('Action');
    80→    },
    81→    { timeout }
    82→  );
    83→}
    84→
    85→module.exports = { waitForEngine, getEngineState, pollEngineState, waitForDashboard };
    86→

     1→'use strict';
     2→/**

    11→ * index.html via page.route() and inject the exposure before the script executes.

    14→ *   1. _getInteractAnim mapping — book/desk/bookshelf→reading, bed/kotatsu/sofa/tv→sit, others→phone

    18→ *   5. All 9 interaction sprites load without network errors
    19→ */
    20→const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');

    26→/**
    27→ * Intercept index.html served at / and inject:
    28→ *   window._gameEngine = engine

    38→      '// ── Initial state (QA injection) ──

window.SimulationEngine = SimulationEngine;'
    39→    );
    40→    await route.fulfill({ response, body });
    41→  });
    42→}
    43→
    44→/**
    45→ * Click the start overlay (if visible) and optionally boost time scale.
    46→ */
    47→async function startEngine(page, timeScale = 20) {
    48→  const overlay = page.locator('#start-overlay');
    49→  if (await overlay.isVisible()) {
    50→    await overlay.click();
    51→  }
    52→  await page.evaluate((scale) => {
    53→    if (window._gameEngine) window._gameEngine.timeScale = scale;
    54→  }, timeScale);
    55→}
    56→
    57→/**
    58→ * Poll character states until predicate returns truthy or timeout.
    59→ * Returns the last character state array that satisfied the predicate.
    60→ */
    61→async function pollCharState(page, predicate, timeoutMs = 45_000, intervalMs = 300) {
    62→  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs;
    63→  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
    64→    const chars = await page.evaluate(() =>
    65→      window._gameEngine.characters.map(c => ({
    66→        id: c.id,
    67→        action: c.action,
    68→        interactAnim: c.interactAnim,
    69→        spriteKey: c.spriteKey,
    70→        targetObjectId: c.targetObjectId,
    71→      }))
    72→    );
    73→    if (predicate(chars)) return chars;
    74→    await page.waitForTimeout(intervalMs);
    75→  }
    76→  throw new Error(`pollCharState timed out after ${timeoutMs}ms`);
    77→}
    78→

    81→test.describe('FRG-243: Contextual Interaction Animations', () => {
    82→
    83→  // ── TEST 1: _getInteractAnim mapping ──────────────────────────────────────
    84→
    85→  test('_getInteractAnim maps object IDs to the correct animation', async ({ page }) => {
    86→    test.setTimeout(30_000);
    87→
    88→    await injectEngineExposure(page);
    89→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
    90→    await page.waitForFunction(() => window.SimulationEngine != null, { timeout: 15_000 });
    91→
    92→    const results = await page.evaluate(() => {
    93→      const fn = window.SimulationEngine._getInteractAnim.bind(window.SimulationEngine);
    94→      return [
    95→        // book / desk / bookshelf → 'reading'
    96→        { id: 'bookshelf_1',       expected: 'reading', actual: fn('bookshelf_1') },
    97→        { id: 'book_closed',       expected: 'reading', actual: fn('book_closed') },
    98→        { id: 'book_open',         expected: 'reading', actual: fn('book_open') },
    99→        { id: 'desk',              expected: 'reading', actual: fn('desk') },
   100→        { id: 'study_desk_north',  expected: 'reading', actual: fn('study_desk_north') },
   101→
   102→        // bed / kotatsu / sofa / tv → 'sit'
   103→        { id: 'bed',               expected: 'sit',     actual: fn('bed') },
   104→        { id: 'kotatsu',           expected: 'sit',     actual: fn('kotatsu') },
   105→        { id: 'living_sofa_left',  expected: 'sit',     actual: fn('living_sofa_left') },
   106→        { id: 'tv',                expected: 'sit',     actual: fn('tv') },
   107→        { id: 'bedroom_bed_main',  expected: 'sit',     actual: fn('bedroom_bed_main') },
   108→
   109→        // all other objects → 'phone'
   110→        { id: 'cafe_espresso',     expected: 'phone',   actual: fn('cafe_espresso') },
   111→        { id: 'fridge',            expected: 'phone',   actual: fn('fridge') },
   112→        { id: 'sink',              expected: 'phone',   actual: fn('sink') },
   113→        { id: 'cash_register',     expected: 'phone',   actual: fn('cash_register') },
   114→        { id: 'easel_blank',       expected: 'phone',   actual: fn('easel_blank') },
   115→      ];
   116→    });
   117→
   118→    for (const r of results) {
   119→      console.log(`_getInteractAnim('${r.id}'): expected=${r.expected}, actual=${r.actual}`);
   120→      expect(r.actual, `_getInteractAnim('${r.id}') should return '${r.expected}'`).toBe(r.expected);
   121→    }
   122→  });
   123→
   124→  // ── TEST 2: spriteKey and interactAnim change during interaction ──────────
   125→
   126→  test('startInteraction sets spriteKey and interactAnim correctly', async ({ page }) => {
   127→    test.setTimeout(30_000);
   128→
   129→    await injectEngineExposure(page);
   130→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   131→    await page.waitForFunction(() => window._gameEngine?.characters?.length === 3, { timeout: 15_000 });
   132→
   133→    const results = await page.evaluate(() => {
   134→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   135→      const chars = engine.characters;
   136→
   137→      const maple = chars.find(c => c.id === 'maple');
   138→      const sol   = chars.find(c => c.id === 'sol');
   139→      const nyx   = chars.find(c => c.id === 'nyx');
   140→
   141→      // Test each character with a different animation type
   142→      maple.startInteraction('bookshelf_1', 'reading');
   143→      sol.startInteraction('kotatsu', 'sit');
   144→      nyx.startInteraction('cafe_espresso', 'phone');
   145→
   146→      return [
   147→        {
   148→          charId: 'maple',
   149→          objectId: 'bookshelf_1',
   150→          anim: 'reading',
   151→          interactAnim: maple.interactAnim,
   152→          spriteKey: maple.spriteKey,
   153→          action: maple.action,
   154→        },
   155→        {
   156→          charId: 'sol',
   157→          objectId: 'kotatsu',
   158→          anim: 'sit',
   159→          interactAnim: sol.interactAnim,
   160→          spriteKey: sol.spriteKey,
   161→          action: sol.action,
   162→        },
   163→        {
   164→          charId: 'nyx',
   165→          objectId: 'cafe_espresso',
   166→          anim: 'phone',
   167→          interactAnim: nyx.interactAnim,
   168→          spriteKey: nyx.spriteKey,
   169→          action: nyx.action,
   170→        },
   171→      ];
   172→    });
   173→
   174→    for (const r of results) {
   175→      console.log(
   176→        `${r.charId}: action=${r.action}, interactAnim=${r.interactAnim}, spriteKey=${r.spriteKey}`
   177→      );
   178→      expect(r.action, `${r.charId} action should be 'interacting'`).toBe('interacting');
   179→      expect(r.interactAnim, `${r.charId} interactAnim should be '${r.anim}'`).toBe(r.anim);
   180→      expect(r.spriteKey, `${r.charId} spriteKey should be '${r.charId}_${r.anim}'`).toBe(`${r.charId}_${r.anim}`);
   181→    }
   182→  });
   183→
   184→  // ── TEST 3: interactAnim clears after timer expires ────────────────────────
   185→
   186→  test('interactAnim clears and spriteKey reverts to idle after interaction ends', async ({ page }) => {
   187→    test.setTimeout(30_000);
   188→
   189→    await injectEngineExposure(page);
   190→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   191→    await page.waitForFunction(() => window._gameEngine?.characters?.length === 3, { timeout: 15_000 });
   192→
   193→    const result = await page.evaluate(() => {
   194→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   195→      const maple = engine.characters.find(c => c.id === 'maple');
   196→
   197→      // Put maple into an interaction
   198→      maple.startInteraction('bookshelf_1', 'reading');
   199→
   200→      const during = {
   201→        action:      maple.action,
   202→        interactAnim: maple.interactAnim,
   203→        spriteKey:   maple.spriteKey,
   204→      };
   205→
   206→      // Advance the engine past the 2000ms interaction timer
   207→      engine._updateCharacters(2001);
   208→
   209→      const after = {
   210→        action:      maple.action,
   211→        interactAnim: maple.interactAnim,
   212→        spriteKey:   maple.spriteKey,
   213→      };
   214→
   215→      return { during, after };
   216→    });
   217→
   218→    // During interaction
   219→    console.log('During interaction:', JSON.stringify(result.during));
   220→    expect(result.during.action).toBe('interacting');
   221→    expect(result.during.interactAnim).toBe('reading');
   222→    expect(result.during.spriteKey).toBe('maple_reading');
   223→
   224→    // After timer expires
   225→    console.log('After timer expiry:', JSON.stringify(result.after));
   226→    expect(result.after.action, 'action should revert to idle').toBe('idle');
   227→    expect(result.after.interactAnim, 'interactAnim should be null after interaction ends').toBeNull();
   228→    expect(result.after.spriteKey, 'spriteKey should revert to maple_idle').toBe('maple_idle');
   229→  });
   230→
   231→  // ── TEST 4: Live sim — natural interaction uses contextual spriteKey ───────
   232→
   233→  test('interacting character uses a contextual spriteKey in the live sim', async ({ page }) => {
   234→    test.setTimeout(90_000);
   235→
   236→    await injectEngineExposure(page);
   237→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   238→    await page.waitForFunction(() => window._gameEngine?.characters?.length === 3, { timeout: 15_000 });
   239→    await startEngine(page, 20);
   240→
   241→    const CONTEXTUAL_SUFFIXES = ['_reading', '_sit', '_phone'];
   242→
   243→    // Poll until any character is interacting with a contextual spriteKey
   244→    const chars = await pollCharState(
   245→      page,
   246→      cs => cs.some(
   247→        c => c.action === 'interacting' &&
   248→             c.interactAnim !== null &&
   249→             CONTEXTUAL_SUFFIXES.some(suffix => c.spriteKey.endsWith(suffix))
   250→      ),
   251→      60_000
   252→    );
   253→
   254→    const interacting = chars.filter(
   255→      c => c.action === 'interacting' &&
   256→           c.interactAnim !== null &&
   257→           CONTEXTUAL_SUFFIXES.some(suffix => c.spriteKey.endsWith(suffix))
   258→    );
   259→
   260→    console.log('Interacting with contextual anim:', interacting.map(c =>
   261→      `${c.id}: spriteKey=${c.spriteKey}, interactAnim=${c.interactAnim}, target=${c.targetObjectId}`
   262→    ).join(' | '));
   263→
   264→    expect(interacting.length, 'At least one character should use a contextual spriteKey').toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
   265→
   266→    for (const c of interacting) {
   267→      expect(
   268→        CONTEXTUAL_SUFFIXES.some(suffix => c.spriteKey.endsWith(suffix)),
   269→        `${c.id} spriteKey '${c.spriteKey}' should end with _reading, _sit, or _phone`
   270→      ).toBe(true);
   271→    }
   272→  });
   273→
   274→  // ── TEST 5: All 9 interaction sprites load without errors ─────────────────
   275→
   276→  test('all 9 interaction sprites load without network errors', async ({ page }) => {
   277→    test.setTimeout(30_000);
   278→
   279→    const EXPECTED_SPRITES = [
   280→      'maple_reading', 'maple_sit', 'maple_phone',
   281→      'sol_reading',   'sol_sit',   'sol_phone',
   282→      'nyx_reading',   'nyx_sit',   'nyx_phone',
   283→    ];
   284→
   285→    const spriteResults = {};
   286→
   287→    page.on('response', response => {
   288→      const url = response.url();
   289→      for (const key of EXPECTED_SPRITES) {
   290→        if (url.includes(`${key}.png`)) {
   291→          spriteResults[key] = response.status();
   292→        }
   293→      }
   294→    });
   295→
   296→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   297→
   298→    // Wait for sprite preload — the preloadSprites() promise resolves before
   299→    // the render loop starts; 5s is ample for a local server
   300→    await page.waitForTimeout(5_000);
   301→
   302→    for (const key of EXPECTED_SPRITES) {
   303→      console.log(`Sprite ${key}.png: status=${spriteResults[key] ?? 'not requested'}`);
   304→      expect(spriteResults[key], `${key}.png should have been requested`).toBeDefined();
   305→      expect(spriteResults[key], `${key}.png should return HTTP 200`).toBe(200);
   306→    }
   307→  });
   308→});

     3→ * REGRESSION — FRG-245
     4→ * Character-to-character collision avoidance.
     5→ *
     6→ * Tests run against the local dev server (http://localhost:5175) which serves
     7→ * the feature/frg-245-character-collision-avoidance branch.
     8→ *
     9→ * window._gameEngine is set unconditionally in scene.js create() so no
    10→ * route injection is needed.
    11→ *
    12→ * Actual API (verified against source):
    13→ *   engine._buildDynamicWalkable(excludeChar)      — clones static grid, marks other chars blocked
    14→ *   engine._findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty, walkable) — returns first free cardinal neighbor
    15→ *   engine._doWander(char)                         — runs wander logic inc. deadlock escape
    16→ *   engine.update(deltaMs)                         — advances one sim tick
    17→ *   char.moveTo(goalTx, goalTy, walkable?)         — A* path on given grid; returns boolean
    18→ *   char._failedMoveCount                          — consecutive wander failures; reset on success
    19→ *   char.wanderTimer                               — ms until next wander attempt
    20→ *   engine.walkable[row][col]                      — static walkable grid (boolean[][])
    21→ *   engine.characters                              — [Maple(Amelia), Sol(Lucy), Nyx(Ash)]
    22→ *   engine.objectEngine.getById(id)                — valid IDs: stove,fridge,tea_set,kotatsu,etc.
    23→ *
    24→ * Walkable grid: 19 cols × 13 rows.
    25→ *   Interior floor: col 1–17, row 2–9 (minus object tiles).
    26→ *   Object tiles (non-walkable): stove(3,3), fridge(2,3), tea_set(5,5), kotatsu(6,6),
    27→ *     tv(9,3), bookshelf(15,3), desk(14,5), bed(16,5), easel(2,7), bonsai(11,8).
    28→ *
    29→ * Test layout:
    30→ *   1. No tile sharing — no two chars idle/interacting on the same tile over 30+ poll samples
    31→ *   2. _buildDynamicWalkable — other chars blocked, own tile walkable, static grid unchanged
    32→ *   3. moveTo with dynamic grid — path routes around a blocking character's tile
    33→ *   4. Deadlock escape — _failedMoveCount resets to 0 after third wander failure
    34→ *   5. Live sim stability — no crashes and all chars become active within 120s sim-time
    35→ */
    36→const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
    37→
    38→const LOCAL_URL = 'http://localhost:5175';
    39→
    40→// ── helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    41→
    42→/**
    43→ * Wait for the SimulationEngine to be fully initialised with 3 characters.
    44→ */
    45→async function waitForEngine(page) {
    46→  await page.waitForFunction(
    47→    () => window._gameEngine?.characters?.length === 3,
    48→    { timeout: 15_000 }
    49→  );
    50→}
    51→
    52→// ── Tests ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    53→

    55→
    56→  // ── TEST 1: No tile sharing during idle/interacting ────────────────────────
    57→
    58→  test('no two characters share a tile when idle or interacting over 30 poll samples', async ({ page }) => {
    59→    test.setTimeout(120_000);
    60→
    61→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
    62→    await waitForEngine(page);
    63→
    64→    // Let the Phaser game loop run naturally; poll character positions.
    65→    // 30 polls × 300 ms = ~9 real seconds of simulation coverage.
    66→    const violations = [];
    67→    const POLL_COUNT   = 30;
    68→    const POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 300;
    69→
    70→    for (let i = 0; i < POLL_COUNT; i++) {
    71→      await page.waitForTimeout(POLL_INTERVAL_MS);
    72→
    73→      const charPositions = await page.evaluate(() =>
    74→        window._gameEngine.characters.map(c => ({
    75→          label:  c.label,
    76→          tx:     Math.round(c.tx),
    77→          ty:     Math.round(c.ty),
    78→          action: c.action,
    79→        }))
    80→      );
    81→
    82→      // Only check when characters are in a stable state (not mid-walk)
    83→      const stable = charPositions.filter(
    84→        c => c.action === 'idle' || c.action === 'interacting' || c.action === 'talking'
    85→      );
    86→
    87→      for (let a = 0; a < stable.length; a++) {
    88→        for (let b = a + 1; b < stable.length; b++) {
    89→          if (stable[a].tx === stable[b].tx && stable[a].ty === stable[b].ty) {
    90→            violations.push({
    91→              poll:    i,
    92→              charA:   stable[a].label,
    93→              charB:   stable[b].label,
    94→              tile:    `(${stable[a].tx},${stable[a].ty})`,
    95→              actions: `${stable[a].action}/${stable[b].action}`,
    96→            });
    97→          }
    98→        }
    99→      }
   100→    }
   101→
   102→    if (violations.length > 0) {
   103→      console.error('Tile-sharing violations:', JSON.stringify(violations, null, 2));
   104→    }
   105→

   107→      `Characters shared tiles on ${violations.length} poll(s): ` +

   234→    ).toBe(false);
   235→
   236→    expect(result.pathLength,
   237→      'Path must have at least one step'
   238→    ).toBeGreaterThan(0);
   239→  });
   240→
   241→  // ── TEST 4: Deadlock escape after 3 wander failures ───────────────────────
   242→
   243→  test('_failedMoveCount resets to 0 after third consecutive wander failure (deadlock escape)', async ({ page }) => {
   244→    test.setTimeout(30_000);
   245→
   246→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   247→    await waitForEngine(page);
   248→
   249→    const result = await page.evaluate(() => {
   250→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   251→      const [maple] = engine.characters;
   252→
   253→      // Place maple in an open area
   254→      maple.tx = 8; maple.ty = 4;
   255→      maple.prevTx = 8; maple.prevTy = 4;
   256→      maple.path = []; maple.moveProgress = 0; maple.action = 'idle';
   257→
   258→      // Seed counter: two previous failures already recorded
   259→      maple._failedMoveCount = 2;
   260→
   261→      // Override moveTo to always return false — simulates all paths blocked
   262→      const originalMoveTo = maple.moveTo.bind(maple);
   263→      let callCount = 0;
   264→      maple.moveTo = function() {
   265→        callCount++;
   266→        return false;
   267→      };
   268→
   269→      const countBefore = maple._failedMoveCount; // 2
   270→
   271→      // _doWander: 15 random-tile attempts all fail → _failedMoveCount 2→3 → escape fires → reset to 0
   272→      engine._doWander(maple);
   273→
   274→      const countAfter = maple._failedMoveCount;
   275→
   276→      // Restore so the engine is not permanently broken
   277→      maple.moveTo = originalMoveTo;
   278→
   279→      return { countBefore, countAfter, callCount };
   280→    });
   281→
   282→    console.log('Deadlock escape result:', JSON.stringify(result));
   283→
   284→    expect(result.countBefore,
   285→      '_failedMoveCount should be 2 before the wander attempt'
   286→    ).toBe(2);
   287→
   288→    expect(result.countAfter,
   289→      'After third wander failure, _failedMoveCount must reset to 0 (deadlock escape fired)'
   290→    ).toBe(0);
   291→
   292→    expect(result.callCount,
   293→      'moveTo should have been called at least once during the wander attempt'
   294→    ).toBeGreaterThan(0);
   295→  });
   296→
   297→  // ── TEST 5: Live sim stability over 120s sim-time ────────────────────────
   298→
   299→  test('no character stays permanently stuck and sim runs without errors over 120s sim-time', async ({ page }) => {
   300→    test.setTimeout(60_000);
   301→
   302→    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);
   303→    await waitForEngine(page);
   304→
   305→    // Drive 120s of sim-time synchronously via engine.update(). Each call advances
   306→    // 5000ms of sim-time; Phaser's rAF loop is blocked during the evaluate() call
   307→    // so there is no double-tick. AI is disabled to avoid network requests.
   308→    const stability = await page.evaluate(() => {
   309→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   310→
   311→      // Disable AI engine so no async LLM decisions fire during the driven ticks
   312→      engine.aiEngine = null;
   313→
   314→      const DELTA = 5000; // ms of sim-time per tick
   315→      const TICKS = 24;   // 24 × 5000ms = 120 sim-seconds
   316→
   317→      // Snapshot initial positions using label (characters have no .id field)
   318→      const initialPos = {};
   319→      for (const c of engine.characters) {
   320→        initialPos[c.label] = { tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty) };
   321→      }
   322→
   323→      // Track whether each character ever left its spawn tile or entered a non-idle state
   324→      const everActive = {};
   325→      for (const c of engine.characters) everActive[c.label] = false;
   326→
   327→      const errors = [];
   328→
   329→      for (let tick = 0; tick < TICKS; tick++) {
   330→        try {
   331→          engine.update(DELTA);
   332→        } catch (e) {
   333→          errors.push({ tick, simMs: tick * DELTA, msg: String(e) });
   334→          break;
   335→        }
   336→
   337→        for (const c of engine.characters) {
   338→          if (!everActive[c.label]) {
   339→            const tx = Math.round(c.tx);
   340→            const ty = Math.round(c.ty);
   341→            if (
   342→              c.action !== 'idle' ||
   343→              tx !== initialPos[c.label].tx ||
   344→              ty !== initialPos[c.label].ty
   345→            ) {
   346→              everActive[c.label] = true;
   347→            }
   348→          }
   349→        }
   350→      }
   351→
   352→      const stuck = Object.entries(everActive)
   353→        .filter(([, active]) => !active)
   354→        .map(([label]) => ({ label, spawn: initialPos[label] }));
   355→
   356→      return { stuck, errors, simMs: TICKS * DELTA };
   357→    });
   358→
   359→    console.log(`Sim ran for ${stability.simMs}ms sim-time`);
   360→    if (stability.errors.length > 0) console.error('Sim errors:', stability.errors);
   361→    if (stability.stuck.length > 0) console.warn('Stuck chars:', stability.stuck);
   362→
   363→    expect(stability.errors.length,
   364→      `Sim threw ${stability.errors.length} error(s): ` +
   365→      stability.errors.map(e => e.msg).join('; ')
   366→    ).toBe(0);
   367→
   368→    expect(stability.stuck.length,
   369→      `${stability.stuck.length} character(s) never left their spawn tile in 120 sim-seconds: ` +
   370→      stability.stuck.map(s => `${s.label}@(${s.spawn.tx},${s.spawn.ty})`).join(', ')
   371→    ).toBe(0);
   372→  });
   373→});
   374→

// ms of sim-time per tick\n   315\u2192      const TICKS = 24;   // 24 \u00d7 5000ms = 120 sim-seconds\n   316\u2192\n   317\u2192      // Snapshot initial positions using label (characters have no .id field)\n   318\u2192      const initialPos = {};\n   319\u2192      for (const c of engine.characters) {\n   320\u2192        initialPos[c.label] = { tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty) };\n   321\u2192      }\n   322\u2192\n   323\u2192      // Track whether each character ever left its spawn tile or entered a non-idle state\n   324\u2192      const everActive = {};\n   325\u2192      for (const c of engine.characters) everActive[c.label] = false;\n   326\u2192\n   327\u2192      const errors = [];\n   328\u2192\n   329\u2192      for (let tick = 0; tick < TICKS; tick++) {\n   330\u2192        try {\n   331\u2192          engine.update(DELTA);\n   332\u2192        } catch (e) {\n   333\u2192          errors.push({ tick, simMs: tick * DELTA, msg: String(e) });\n   334\u2192          break;\n   335\u2192        }\n   336\u2192\n   337\u2192        for (const c of engine.characters) {\n   338\u2192          if (!everActive[c.label]) {\n   339\u2192            const tx = Math.round(c.tx);\n   340\u2192            const ty = Math.round(c.ty);\n   341\u2192            if (\n   342\u2192              c.action !== 'idle' ||\n   343\u2192              tx !== initialPos[c.label].tx ||\n   344\u2192              ty !== initialPos[c.label].ty\n   345\u2192            ) {\n   346\u2192              everActive[c.label] = true;\n   347\u2192            }\n   348\u2192          }\n   349\u2192        }\n   350\u2192      }\n   351\u2192\n   352\u2192      const stuck = Object.entries(everActive)\n   353\u2192        .filter(([, active]) => !active)\n   354\u2192        .map(([label]) => ({ label, spawn: initialPos[label] }));\n   355\u2192\n   356\u2192      return { stuck, errors, simMs: TICKS * DELTA };\n   357\u2192    });\n   358\u2192\n   359\u2192    console.log(`Sim ran for ${stability.simMs}ms sim-time`);\n   360\u2192    if (stability.errors.length > 0) console.error('Sim errors:', stability.errors);\n   361\u2192    if (stability.stuck.length > 0) console.warn('Stuck chars:', stability.stuck);\n   362\u2192\n   363\u2192    expect(stability.errors.length,\n   364\u2192      `Sim threw ${stability.errors.length} error(s): ` +\n   365\u2192      stability.errors.map(e => e.msg).join(';    225→      },
   226→    },
   227→  },
   228→];
   229→
   230→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   231→
   232→class ObjectInstance {
   233→  constructor(def) {
   234→    this.id          = def.id;
   235→    this.name        = def.name;
   236→    this.label       = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   237→    this.position    = def.position;
   238→    this.tx          = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   239→    this.ty          = def.position.ty;
   240→    this.states      = def.states;
   241→    this.state       = def.state || 'idle';
   242→    this.interactAnim = def.interactAnim || null;
   243→    this.interactMs  = def.interactMs || 8000;
   244→    this.spriteMap   = def.spriteMap || null;
   245→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   246→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   247→
   248→    // Slot system
   249→    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;
   250→    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object
   251→    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting
   252→  }
   253→
   254→  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */
   255→  isFull() {
   256→    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;
   257→  }
   258→
   259→  /**
   260→   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.
   261→   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.
   262→   */
   263→  reserve(charName) {
   264→    if (this.isFull()) return false;
   265→    this._reservations.add(charName);
   266→    return true;
   267→  }
   268→
   269→  /**
   270→   * Called when charName arrives at the object.
   271→   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.
   272→   */
   273→  arrive(charName) {
   274→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   275→    this._occupants.add(charName);
   276→  }
   277→
   278→  /**
   279→   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.
   280→   * Warns if charName was not a known occupant or reservation — signals an orphaned slot.
   281→   */
   282→  release(charName) {
   283→    if (!this._reservations.has(charName) && !this._occupants.has(charName)) {
   284→      console.warn(
   285→        `[objects] release('${this.id}', '${charName}'): ` +
   286→        `not a known occupant or reservation — possible orphaned slot`
   287→      );
   288→    }
   289→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   290→    this._occupants.delete(charName);
   291→  }
   292→
   293→  /** Returns the names of characters who have reserved a slot (walking toward this object). */
   294→  getReservations() { return Array.from(this._reservations); }
   295→
   296→  /** Returns the names of characters who are actively occupying a slot. */
   297→  getOccupants() { return Array.from(this._occupants); }
   298→
   299→  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */
   300→  clearSlots() {
   301→    this._reservations.clear();
   302→    this._occupants.clear();
   303→  }
   304→
   305→  /**
   306→   * Returns current slot occupancy info.
   307→   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}
   308→   */
   309→  getSlotInfo() {
   310→    return {
   311→      capacity:  this.capacity,
   312→      reserved:  this._reservations.size,
   313→      occupied:  this._occupants.size,
   314→      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,
   315→    };
   316→  }
   317→
   318→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   319→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   320→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   321→  }
   322→
   323→  /**
   324→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   325→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   326→   */
   327→  interact(action = 'use') {
   328→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   329→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   330→    if (!tr) return null;
   331→
   332→    this.state = tr.next;
   333→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   334→
   335→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   336→    return {
   337→      objectId:  this.id,
   338→      state:     this.state,
   339→      speech:    ns?.speech || null,
   340→      emoji:     ns?.emoji  || null,
   341→      spriteKey: this.spriteMap?.[this.state] ?? null,
   342→    };
   343→  }
   344→
   345→  /**
   346→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   347→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   348→   */
   349→  tick(deltaMs) {
   350→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   351→
   352→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   353→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   354→
   355→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   356→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   357→
   358→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   359→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   360→
   361→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   362→    return {
   363→      objectId:  this.id,
   364→      state:     this.state,
   365→      emoji:     ns?.emoji || null,
   366→      auto:      true,
   367→      spriteKey: this.spriteMap?.[this.state] ?? null,
   368→    };
   369→  }
   370→}
   371→
   372→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   373→
   374→export class ObjectEngine {
   375→  constructor() {
   376→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   377→  }
   378→
   379→  addObjects(defs) {
   380→    for (const def of defs) {
   381→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   382→    }
   383→  }
   384→
   385→  /**
   386→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   387→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   388→   */
   389→  tick(deltaMs) {
   390→    const events = [];
   391→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   392→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   393→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   394→    }
   395→    return events;
   396→  }
   397→
   398→  /**
   399→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   400→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   401→   */
   402→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   403→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   404→  }
   405→
   406→  getAll()    { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   407→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   408→
   409→  reserve(objectId, charName) { return this._map.get(objectId)?.reserve(charName) ?? false; }
   410→  arrive(objectId, charName)  { this._map.get(objectId)?.arrive(charName); }
   411→  release(objectId, charName) { this._map.get(objectId)?.release(charName); }
   412→  clearSlots(objectId)        { this._map.get(objectId)?.clearSlots(); }
   413→  clearAllSlots()             { for (const obj of this._map.values()) obj.clearSlots(); }
   414→}
   415→

    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    50→    const r = [];
    51→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    52→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    53→    }
    54→    grid.push(r);
    55→  }
    56→  // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
    57→  for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
    58→    const { tx, ty } = def.position;
    59→    if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}

   212→  }

   216→  update(_time, delta) {
   217→    this.engine.update(delta);
   218→    this.clockText.setText(this.engine.getSimTimeString());
   219→
   220→    // Show speech bubbles queued by the engine
   221→    for (const char of this.engine.characters) {
   222→      if (char.pendingSpeech && char.sprite) {
   223→        showSpeech(this, char.sprite, char.pendingSpeech);
   224→        char.pendingSpeech = null;
   225→      }
   226→    }
   227→
   228→    // Process object state-transition events: swap sprites and float emojis
   229→    if (this.engine.pendingEvents.length > 0) {

   231→        const obj = this.engine.objectEngine.getById(ev.objectId);
   232→        if (!obj) continue;
   233→

   235→        if (ev.spriteKey && this._objectSprites[ev.objectId]) {
   236→          this._objectSprites[ev.objectId].setTexture(ev.spriteKey);
   237→        }
   238→
   239→        // Float emoji above the object
   240→        if (ev.emoji) {
   241→          const px = obj.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   242→          const py = obj.ty * TILE_SIZE;
   243→          const label = this.add.text(px, py, ev.emoji, { fontSize: '24px' }).setDepth(25);
   244→          this.tweens.add({
   245→            targets: label,
   246→            y:       label.y - 40,
   247→            alpha:   0,
   248→            duration: 2000,
   249→            onComplete: () => label.destroy(),
   250→          });
   251→        }
   252→      }
   253→      this.engine.pendingEvents = [];
   254→    }
   255→  }

   143→<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/phaser@3.88.2/dist/phaser.min.js"></script>
   144→<script type="module">
   145→import { CafeScene } from './src/scene.js?v=15';
   146→new Phaser.Game({
   147→  type: Phaser.AUTO,
   148→  width: 912, height: 642,
   149→  backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e',
   150→  scale: { mode: Phaser.Scale.FIT, autoCenter: Phaser.Scale.CENTER_BOTH },
   151→  render: { antialias: false, pixelArt: true },
   152→  scene: CafeScene,
   153→});
   154→</script>
   155→
   156→<!-- ── Debug toggle button ── -->
   157→<button id="debug-toggle">Debug</button>
   158→
   159→<!-- ── Debug overlay panel ── -->
   160→<div id="debug-panel">
   161→  <div id="debug-panel-header">
   162→    <span>OBJECT STATES</span>
   163→    <span id="debug-clock">—</span>
   164→  </div>
   165→  <div id="debug-panel-body">
   166→    <div id="dp-objects"></div>
   167→  </div>
   168→  <div id="debug-panel-footer">
   169→    <a href="debug.html" target="_blank">&#8599; Full dashboard</a>
   170→  </div>
   171→</div>
   172→
   173→<script>
   174→(function() {
   175→  const toggle  = document.getElementById('debug-toggle');
   176→  const panel   = document.getElementById('debug-panel');
   177→  const dpObjs  = document.getElementById('dp-objects');
   178→  const dpClock = document.getElementById('debug-clock');
   179→
   180→  let open = false;
   181→  let rafId = null;
   182→
   183→  const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   184→    'cooking','brewing','painting','working','tending','reading','on',
   185→  ]);
   186→  const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done','ready','open','cozy','resting']);
   187→
   188→  function badgeCls(state) {
   189→    if (state === 'idle')          return 'idle';
   190→    if (DONE_STATES.has(state))    return 'done';
   191→    if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state))  return 'active';
   192→    return 'other';
   193→  }
   194→
   195→  // Build DOM for each object row once, then update in place
   196→  let built = false;
   197→
   198→  function buildRows(objects) {
   199→    dpObjs.innerHTML = '';
   200→    for (const obj of objects) {
   201→      const row = document.createElement('div');
   202→      row.innerHTML = `
   203→        <div class="dp-obj" id="dpo-${obj.id}">
   204→          <span class="dp-obj-name">${obj.name}</span>
   205→          <span class="dp-badge" id="dpbadge-${obj.id}"></span>
   206→          <span id="dptimer-${obj.id}"></span>
   207→        </div>
   208→        <div class="dp-timer" id="dptbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   209→          <div class="dp-timer-fill" id="dptfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   210→        </div>
   211→      `;
   212→      dpObjs.appendChild(row);
   213→    }
   214→    built = true;
   215→  }
   216→
   217→  function updateRows(engine) {
   218→    const objects = engine.objectEngine.getAll();
   219→    if (!built) buildRows(objects);
   220→
   221→    dpClock.textContent = engine.getSimTimeString();
   222→
   223→    for (const obj of objects) {
   224→      const badge = document.getElementById(`dpbadge-${obj.id}`);
   225→      const tbar  = document.getElementById(`dptbar-${obj.id}`);
   226→      const tfill = document.getElementById(`dptfill-${obj.id}`);
   227→      const tspan = document.getElementById(`dptimer-${obj.id}`);
   228→      if (!badge) continue;
   229→
   230→      // Badge
   231→      if (badge.dataset.state !== obj.state) {
   232→        badge.textContent    = obj.state;
   233→        badge.className      = `dp-badge ${badgeCls(obj.state)}`;
   234→        badge.dataset.state  = obj.state;
   235→
   236→        // Rebuild use button
   237→        const existing = tspan.previousSibling;
   238→        // We rebuild via innerHTML of tspan for the button
   239→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   240→        const actions  = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   241→        tspan.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   242→          `<button class="dp-btn" onclick="window._dpInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   243→        ).join('');
   244→      }
   245→
   246→      // Timer bar
   247→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   248→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   249→      if (hasTimer) {
   250→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   251→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   252→        tbar.style.display  = '';
   253→        tfill.style.width   = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   254→      } else {
   255→        tbar.style.display = 'none';
   256→      }
   257→    }
   258→  }
   259→
   260→  window._dpInteract = function(id, action) {
   261→    if (!window._gameEngine) return;
   262→    window._gameEngine.objectEngine.interact(id, action);
   263→  };
   264→
   265→  function renderLoop() {
   266→    if (!open) { rafId = null; return; }
   267→    if (window._gameEngine) updateRows(window._gameEngine);
   268→    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);
   269→  }
   270→
   271→  toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
   272→    open = !open;
   273→    toggle.classList.toggle('open', open);
   274→    toggle.textContent = open ? 'Debug ✕' : 'Debug';
   275→    panel.classList.toggle('visible', open);
   276→    if (open && !rafId) {
   277→      built = false; // rebuild rows on open in case engine wasn't ready before
   278→      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);
   279→    }
   280→  });
   281→})();
   282→</script>
   283→</body>
   284→</html>
   285→

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        buildDynamicWalkable: (char) => this._buildDynamicWalkable(char),
    56→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    57→      });
    58→    }
    59→
    60→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    61→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    62→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    63→      if (ev.emoji || ev.spriteKey) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    64→    }
    65→
    66→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    67→      // Defensive release: if interactTarget is set but the character is no longer
    68→      // interacting, an external change (e.g. a stale async AI decision resolving
    69→      // between frames) moved them out of 'interacting' without triggering the
    70→      // normal detection below.  Release the slot now so the object doesn't stay
    71→      // permanently full.
    72→      if (char.interactTarget && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    73→        console.warn(
    74→          `[Engine] defensive release: ${char.name} has interactTarget ` +
    75→          `'${char.interactTarget}' but action='${char.action}' — releasing slot`
    76→        );
    77→        this.objectEngine.release(char.interactTarget, char.name);
    78→        char.interactTarget = null;
    79→      }
    80→

   115→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
   116→        }
   117→      }
   118→
   119→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
   120→      char.update(deltaMs);
   121→
   122→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
   123→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
   124→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
   125→      }
   126→    }
   127→  }
   128→
   129→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   130→
   131→  /**
   132→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   133→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   134→   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.
   135→   */
   136→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   137→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   138→    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';
   139→
   140→    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.
   141→    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.
   142→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   143→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   144→
   145→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   146→
   147→    if (event) {
   148→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   149→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   150→
   151→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   152→
   153→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   154→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   155→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   156→      if (obj && event.state) {
   157→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   158→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   159→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   160→        }
   161→      }
   162→
   163→      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction
   164→      if (obj) {
   165→        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   166→        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   167→        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   168→          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   169→        } else {
   170→          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   171→        }
   172→      }
   173→
   174→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs, obj?.interactAnim ?? null);
   175→
   176→      if (event.speech)    char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   177→      if (event.emoji || event.spriteKey) this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   178→    } else {
   179→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   180→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.
   181→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   182→      this._fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, objectId);
   183→    }
   184→  }
   185→
   186→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   187→
   188→  /**
   189→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   190→   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.
   191→   */
   192→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   193→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   194→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   195→
   196→    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.
   197→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   198→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   199→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   200→
   201→    if (dist > 3) {
   202→      // Target has drifted — try to follow if not too far
   203→      if (dist <= 10) {
   204→        const dynWalkable = this._buildDynamicWalkable(char);
   205→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty), dynWalkable);
   206→        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty, dynWalkable)) {
   207→          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival
   208→          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   209→          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;
   210→          return;
   211→        }
   212→      }
   213→      // Too far or unreachable — abort
   214→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   215→        type:      'fallback',
   216→        charLabel: char.label,
   217→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   218→        fromLabel: target.label,
   219→        toLabel:   null,
   220→      });
   221→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   222→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   223→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   224→      return;
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   228→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   229→
   230→    if (!canTalk) {
   231→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   232→        type:           'talk_rejected',
   233→        initiatorLabel: char.label,
   234→        targetLabel:    target.label,
   235→      });
   236→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   237→      return;
   238→    }
   239→
   240→    this._startConversation(char, target);
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  /**
   244→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   245→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   246→   */
   247→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   248→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   249→  }
   250→
   251→  /**
   252→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   253→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   254→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   255→   */
   256→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   257→    // Release any pending object reservation charB held while walking.
   258→    // startTalk() clears targetObjectId without calling objectEngine.release(),
   259→    // so we must do it here before the slot becomes permanently orphaned.
   260→    if (charB.targetObjectId) {
   261→      this.objectEngine.release(charB.targetObjectId, charB.name);
   262→      charB.targetObjectId = null;
   263→      charB.pendingAction  = null;
   264→    }
   265→
   266→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   267→
   268→    // Face each other
   269→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   270→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   271→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   272→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   273→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   274→    } else {
   275→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   276→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   277→    }
   278→
   279→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles

easel.autoTimer = 1;\n      const easelPaintingToDoneEv = easel.tick(100); // painting \u2192 done\n\n      // \u2500\u2500 fridge (no spriteMap): open \u2192 idle (via tick) \u2500\u2500\n      const creates _objectSprites for mapped objects at depth=1 with origin(0,0) and idle texture', async ({ page }) => {\n    test.setTimeout(30_000);\n\n    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);\n    await window.Phaser?.GAMES?.[0]?.scene?.scenes?.[0];\n      if (!scene || !scene._objectSprites) {\n        return { error: '_objectSprites not found on scene' };\n      }\n\n      const TILE_SIZE = 48;\n      const spriteIds = Object.keys(scene._objectSprites);\n\n      const details = {};\n      for (const id of spriteIds) {\n        const img = scene._objectSprites[id];\n        const engine = window._gameEngine;\n        const obj = engine.objectEngine.getById(id);\n        const expectedX = obj?.tx != null ? obj.tx * TILE_SIZE : null;\n        const expectedY = obj?.ty != null ? obj.ty * TILE_SIZE : null;\n        details[id] = {\n          textureKey: img.texture?.key,\n          depth:      img.depth,\n          originX:    img.originX,\n          originY:    img.originY,\n          x:          img.x,\n          y:          img.y,\n          expectedX,\n          expectedY,\n        };\n      }\n\n      return { spriteIds, details };\n    });\n\n    console.log('_objectSprites result:', JSON.stringify(result, null, 2));\n\n    // Should not have an error\n    expect(result.error, result.error).toBeUndefined();\n\n    // All 4 mapped objects must have sprite entries\n    const MAPPED_IDS = ['stove', 'tea_set', 'bookshelf', 'easel'];\n    for (const id of MAPPED_IDS) {\n      expect(result.spriteIds, `_objectSprites should contain '${id}'`).toContain(id);\n    }\n\n    // No entries for unmapped objects\n    const UNMAPPED_IDS = ['fridge', 'kotatsu', 'bonsai', 'desk', 'bed', 'tv'];\n    for (const id of UNMAPPED_IDS) {\n      expect(result.spriteIds, `_objectSprites expect(d.depth,   `${id} sprite depth should be 1`).toBe(1);\n      expect(d.originX, `${id} sprite originX should be 0`).toBe(0);\n      expect(d.originY, `${id} sprite originY should be 0`).toBe(0);\n      expect(d.textureKey,\n        `${id} initial texture should be the idle sprite '${EXPECTED_IDLE_SPRITES[id]}'`\n      ).toBe(EXPECTED_IDLE_SPRITES[id]);\n      // Position should match object tile * TILE_SIZE\n      expect(d.x, `${id} sprite x should be tx*48`).toBe(d.expectedX);\n      expect(d.y, `${id} sprite y should be ty*48`).toBe(d.expectedY);\n    }\n  });\n\n  // \u2500\u2500 TEST 5: Sprite texture swaps on state transition (live sim) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n  test('_objectSprites texture swaps on state transition and reverts to idle on return', async ({ page }) => {\n    test.setTimeout(30_000);\n\n    await page.goto(LOCAL_URL);\n    await waitForEngine(page);\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500); // let Phaser create() complete\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 5a: Check initial textures \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    const initialTextures = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const scene = window.Phaser?.GAMES?.[0]?.scene?.scenes?.[0];\n      return {\n        stove: texture').toBe('book_closed');\n    expect(initialTextures.easel,     'easel initial texture').toBe('easel_blank');\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 5b: Trigger interact \u2192 cooking, push spriteKey event to pendingEvents \u2500\u2500\n    await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const engine = window._gameEngine;\n      // Interact with stove: idle \u2192 cooking\n      const ev = engine.objectEngine.interact('stove', 'use');\n      // Push the event so scene.update() picks it up on the next RAF\n      if (ev) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev);\n    });\n\n    // Wait for Phaser's RAF loop to call scene.update() and process pendingEvents\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500);\n\n    const afterCookingTexture = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const scene = window.Phaser?.GAMES?.[0]?.scene?.scenes?.[0];\n      return scene._objectSprites?.stove?.texture?.key;\n    });\n\n    console.log('Stove texture after idle\u2192cooking interact:', through done \u2192 idle, verify texture reverts \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const engine = window._gameEngine;\n      const stove = engine.objectEngine.getById('stove');\n\n      // Fast-forward: cooking \u2192 done via auto timer\n      stove.autoTimer = 1;\n      const ev1 = stove.tick(100); // cooking \u2192 done (spriteKey: 'stove_on', same visual)\n      if (ev1?.spriteKey) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev1);\n\n      // Fast-forward: done \u2192 idle via auto timer\n      stove.autoTimer = 1;\n      const ev2 = stove.tick(100); // done \u2192 idle (spriteKey: 'stove_off')\n      if (ev2?.spriteKey) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev2);\n    });\n\n    // Wait for RAF to process both events\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500);\n\n    const afterIdleTexture = await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const scene = window.Phaser?.GAMES?.[0]?.scene?.scenes?.[0];\n      return scene._objectSprites?.stove?.texture?.key;\n    });\n\n    console.log('Stove texture after returning to idle:', afterIdleTexture);\n    expect(afterIdleTexture,\n      'stove texture should revert to stove_off after returning to idle'\n    ).toBe('stove_off');\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 5d: Verify bookshelf swap (idle\u2192reading\u2192idle) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    await page.evaluate(() => {\n      const engine = window._gameEngine;\n      const bookshelf = engine.objectEngine.getById('bookshelf');\n\n      // idle \u2192 reading\n      const ev1 = bookshelf.interact('use');\n      if    420→    expect(initialTextures.tea_set,   'tea_set initial texture').toBe('cup_empty');
   421→    expect(initialTextures.bookshelf, 'bookshelf initial texture').toBe('book_closed');
   422→    expect(initialTextures.easel,     'easel initial texture').toBe('easel_blank');
   423→
   424→    // ── 5b: Trigger interact → cooking, push spriteKey event to pendingEvents ──
   425→    await page.evaluate(() => {
   426→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   427→      // Interact with stove: idle → cooking
   428→      const ev = engine.objectEngine.interact('stove', 'use');
   429→      // Push the event so scene.update() picks it up on the next RAF
   430→      if (ev) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev);
   431→    });
   432→
   433→    // Wait for Phaser's RAF loop to call scene.update() and process pendingEvents
   434→    await page.waitForTimeout(500);
   435→
   436→    const afterCookingTexture = await page.evaluate(() => {
   437→      const scene = window.Phaser?.GAMES?.[0]?.scene?.scenes?.[0];
   438→      return scene._objectSprites?.stove?.texture?.key;
   439→    });
   440→
   441→    console.log('Stove texture after idle→cooking interact:', afterCookingTexture);
   442→    expect(afterCookingTexture,
   443→      'stove texture should be stove_on after transitioning to cooking'
   444→    ).toBe('stove_on');
   445→
   446→    // ── 5c: Auto-tick stove through done → idle, verify texture reverts ────────
   447→    await page.evaluate(() => {
   448→      const engine = window._gameEngine;
   449→      const stove = engine.objectEngine.getById('stove');
   450→
   451→      // Fast-forward: cooking → done via auto timer
   452→      stove.autoTimer = 1;
   453→      const ev1 = stove.tick(100); // cooking → done (spriteKey: 'stove_on', same visual)
   454→      if (ev1?.spriteKey) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev1);
   455→
   456→      // Fast-forward: done → idle via auto timer
   457→      stove.autoTimer = 1;
   458→      const ev2 = stove.tick(100); // done → idle (spriteKey: 'stove_off')
   459→      if (ev2?.spriteKey) engine.pendingEvents.push(ev2);
   460→    });

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #119
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `tests/regression/object-sprite-swap.spec.js` — new 5-test regression suite for FRG-246 (object sprite swap on state transition), targeting `localhost:5176` ## Key Decisions - **Route injection for scene access**: Tests 4 and 5 need `_objectSprites` from the `CafeScene` instance. Since `window._gameEngine` only exposes the engine (not the scene), I intercept `scene.js` via `page.route()` to inject `window._gameScene = this` after `window._gameEngine = this.engine` — matching the injection pattern used in `contextual-interaction-animations.spec.js`. - **Direct event push for live swap test**: Test 5 triggers `objectEngine.interact()` directly and manually pushes the returned event into `engine.pendingEvents`, then waits 500ms for Phaser's RAF loop to call `scene.update()` and process it — cleaner than trying to drive the full game loop. - **Port 5176**: Chosen sequentially after the 5175 used by FRG-245, served via `npx serve` from the cloned source repo (no package.json in source). ## PR / Branch - Pushed directly to `main` per project convention.
▶ VIEW RAW DATA 
{
  "content": {
    "type": "text",
    "text": "## Status\nDONE\n\n## What Changed\n- `tests/regression/object-sprite-swap.spec.js` \u2014 new 5-test regression suite for FRG-246 (object sprite swap on state transition), targeting `localhost:5176`\n\n## Key Decisions\n- **Route injection for scene access**: Tests 4 and 5 need `_objectSprites` from the `CafeScene` instance. Since `window._gameEngine` only exposes the engine (not the scene), I intercept `scene.js` via `page.route()` to inject `window._gameScene = this` after `window._gameEngine = this.engine` \u2014 matching the injection pattern used in `contextual-interaction-animations.spec.js`.\n- **Direct event push for live swap test**: Test 5 triggers `objectEngine.interact()` directly and manually pushes the returned event into `engine.pendingEvents`, then waits 500ms for Phaser's RAF loop to call `scene.update()` and process it \u2014 cleaner than trying to drive the full game loop.\n- **Port 5176**: Chosen sequentially after the 5175 used by FRG-245, served via `npx serve` from the cloned source repo (no package.json in source).\n\n## PR / Branch\n- Pushed directly to `main` per project convention."
